findDispatchQueueToBoundLocked examines queues in round robin order and\n// returns the one with minimum virtual finish time of the oldest waiting request.\n// Uses anti-windup mechanism to prevent queue from advancing ahead of arrivals.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) findDispatchQueueToBoundLocked() (*queue, *request) {\n\tminVirtualFinish := fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds\n\tsMin := fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds\n\tdsMin := fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds\n\tsMax := fqrequest.MinSeatSeconds\n\tdsMax := fqrequest.MinSeatSeconds\n\tvar minQueue *queue\n\tvar minIndex int\n\tnq := len(qs.queues)\n\t\n\tfor range qs.queues {\n\t\tqs.robinIndex = (qs.robinIndex + 1) % nq\n\t\tqueue := qs.queues[qs.robinIndex]\n\t\toldestWaiting, _ := queue.requestsWaiting.Peek()\n\t\t\n\t\tif oldestWaiting != nil {\n\t\t\tsMin = min(sMin, queue.nextDispatchR)\n\t\t\tsMax = max(sMax, queue.nextDispatchR)\n\t\t\testimatedWorkInProgress := fqrequest.SeatsTimesDuration(float64(queue.seatsInUse), \n\t\t\t\tqs.estimatedServiceDuration)\n\t\t\tdsMin = min(dsMin, queue.nextDispatchR-estimatedWorkInProgress)\n\t\t\tdsMax = max(dsMax, queue.nextDispatchR-estimatedWorkInProgress)\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t// Virtual finish time of oldest request in this queue\n\t\t\tcurrentVirtualFinish := queue.nextDispatchR + oldestWaiting.totalWork()\n\t\t\tklog.V(11).InfoS(\"Considering queue to dispatch\", \"queueSet\", qs.qCfg.Name, \n\t\t\t\t\"queue\", qs.robinIndex, \"finishR\", currentVirtualFinish)\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\tif currentVirtualFinish < minVirtualFinish {\n\t\t\t\tminVirtualFinish = currentVirtualFinish\n\t\t\t\tminQueue = queue\n\t\t\t\tminIndex = qs.robinIndex\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\toldestReqFromMinQueue, _ := minQueue.requestsWaiting.Peek()\n\tif oldestReqFromMinQueue == nil {\n\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"selected queue is empty\"), \"Impossible\", \"queueSet\", qs.qCfg.Name)\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\t\n\tif !qs.canAccommodateSeatsLocked(oldestReqFromMinQueue.MaxSeats()) {\n\t\tklogV := klog.V(4)\n\t\tif klogV.Enabled() {\n\t\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s): request %v %v seats %d cannot be dispatched from queue %d, \"+\n\t\t\t\t\"waiting for currently executing requests to complete, %d requests are occupying %d seats and the limit is %d\",\n\t\t\t\tqs.qCfg.Name, oldestReqFromMinQueue.descr1, oldestReqFromMinQueue.descr2, \n\t\t\t\toldestReqFromMinQueue.MaxSeats(), minQueue.index, qs.totRequestsExecuting, \n\t\t\t\tqs.totSeatsInUse, qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)\n\t\t}\n\t\tmetrics.AddDispatchWithNoAccommodation(qs.qCfg.Name, oldestReqFromMinQueue.fsName)\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\t\n\toldestReqFromMinQueue.removeFromQueueLocked()\n\n\t// If the requested final seats exceed capacity, reduce them and adjust latency\n\tif oldestReqFromMinQueue.workEstimate.FinalSeats > uint64(qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit) {\n\t\tfinalSeats := uint64(qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)\n\t\tadditionalLatency := oldestReqFromMinQueue.workEstimate.finalWork.DurationPerSeat(float64(finalSeats))\n\t\toldestReqFromMinQueue.workEstimate.FinalSeats = finalSeats\n\t\toldestReqFromMinQueue.workEstimate.AdditionalLatency = additionalLatency\n\t}\n\n\t// Round-robin indexing starts at chosen queue for next round\n\tqs.robinIndex = minIndex\n\n\tif minQueue.nextDispatchR < oldestReqFromMinQueue.arrivalR {\n\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"dispatch before arrival\"), \"Inconceivable!\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \n\t\t\t\"queue\", minQueue.index, \"dispatchR\", minQueue.nextDispatchR, \"request\", oldestReqFromMinQueue)\n\t}\n\tmetrics.SetDispatchMetrics(qs.qCfg.Name, qs.currentR.ToFloat(), minQueue.nextDispatchR.ToFloat(), \n\t\tsMin.ToFloat(), sMax.ToFloat(), dsMin.ToFloat(), dsMax.ToFloat())\n\treturn minQueue, oldestReqFromMinQueue\n}\n```\n\n#### Anti-Windup Mechanism (boundNextDispatchLocked):\n\n```go\n// boundNextDispatchLocked applies the anti-windup hack.\n// We need a hack because all non-empty queues are allocated the same\n// number of seats. A queue that can not use all those seats and does\n// not go empty accumulates a progressively earlier `nextDispatchR` compared\n// to queues that are using more than they are allocated.\n// This insists that dispatch in the virtual world not precede arrival.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) boundNextDispatchLocked(queue *queue) {\n\toldestReqFromMinQueue, _ := queue.requestsWaiting.Peek()\n\tif oldestReqFromMinQueue == nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tvar virtualStartBound = oldestReqFromMinQueue.arrivalR\n\tif queue.nextDispatchR < virtualStartBound {\n\t\tif klogV := klog.V(4); klogV.Enabled() {\n\t\t\tklogV.InfoS(\"AntiWindup tweaked queue\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"queue\", queue.index, \n\t\t\t\t\"time\", qs.clock.Now().Format(nsTimeFmt), \"requestDescr1\", oldestReqFromMinQueue.descr1, \n\t\t\t\t\"requestDescr2\", oldestReqFromMinQueue.descr2, \"newVirtualStart\", virtualStartBound, \n\t\t\t\t\"deltaVirtualStart\", (virtualStartBound - queue.nextDispatchR))\n\t\t}\n\t\tqueue.nextDispatchR = virtualStartBound\n\t}\n}\n```\n\n#### Request Finishing and Borrowing:\n\n```go\n// finishRequestLocked is called when a previously dispatched request completes\nfunc (qs *queueSet) finishRequestLocked(r *request) {\n\tnow := qs.clock.Now()\n\tqs.totRequestsExecuting--\n\tmetrics.AddRequestsExecuting(r.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, r.fsName, -1)\n\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsExecuting.Add(-1)\n\n\tactualServiceDuration := now.Sub(r.startTime)\n\n\treleaseSeatsLocked := func() {\n\t\tdefer qs.removeQueueIfEmptyLocked(r)\n\n\t\tqs.totSeatsInUse -= r.MaxSeats()\n\t\tmetrics.AddSeatConcurrencyInUse(qs.qCfg.Name, r.fsName, -r.MaxSeats())\n\t\tqs.execSeatsGauge.Add(-float64(r.MaxSeats()))\n\t\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n\t\tif r.queue != nil {\n\t\t\tr.queue.seatsInUse -= r.MaxSeats()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tklogV := klog.V(6)\n\t\tif r.workEstimate.AdditionalLatency <= 0 {\n\t\t\t// Release seats immediately\n\t\t\treleaseSeatsLocked()\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Handle additional latency (final work phase)\n\t\t// Linger on FinalSeats for AdditionalLatency duration\n\t\tqs.clock.EventAfterDuration(func(_ time.Time) {\n\t\t\tqs.lockAndSyncTime(r.ctx)\n\t\t\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n\t\t\tnow := qs.clock.Now()\n\t\t\treleaseSeatsLocked()\n\t\t\tqs.dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked()\n\t\t}, r.workEstimate.AdditionalLatency)\n\t}()\n\n\tif r.queue != nil {\n\t\t// Request has finished, remove from requests executing\n\t\tr.queue.requestsExecuting = r.queue.requestsExecuting.Delete(r)\n\n\t\t// When a request finishes being served with actual service time S,\n\t\t// the queue's nextDispatchR is decremented by (G - S)*width.\n\t\t// G is estimatedServiceDuration, S is actual, width is InitialSeats\n\t\tr.queue.nextDispatchR -= fqrequest.SeatsTimesDuration(float64(r.InitialSeats()), \n\t\t\tqs.estimatedServiceDuration-actualServiceDuration)\n\t\tqs.boundNextDispatchLocked(r.queue)\n\t} else {\n\t\tqs.requestsExecutingSet = qs.requestsExecutingSet.Delete(r)\n\t}\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 2. **types.go** - Data Structures\n\n```go\n// request is a temporary container for requests with additional\n// tracking fields required for QueueSet functionality\ntype request struct {\n\tctx context.Context\n\tqs *queueSet\n\tflowDistinguisher string\n\tfsName            string\n\n\t// The relevant queue. Is nil if this request did not go through a queue\n\tqueue *queue\n\n\t// estimated amount of work of the request\n\tworkEstimate completedWorkEstimate\n\n\t// decision gets set to a `requestDecision` indicating what to do\n\t// with this request. It gets set exactly once, when the request\n\t// is removed from its queue. The value will be decisionReject,\n\t// decisionCancel, or decisionExecute.\n\t//\n\t// decision.Set is called with the queueSet locked.\n\t// decision.Get is called without the queueSet locked.\n\tdecision promise.WriteOnce\n\n\t// arrivalTime is the real time when the request entered this system\n\tarrivalTime time.Time\n\n\t// descr1 and descr2 are not used in any logic but they appear in log messages\n\tdescr1, descr2 interface{}\n\n\tqueueNoteFn fq.QueueNoteFn\n\n\t// The preceding fields are filled in at creation and not modified since;\n\t// the following fields may be modified later and must only be accessed while\n\t// holding the queueSet's lock.\n\n\t// Removes this request from its queue. If the request is not put into a queue it will be nil.\n\tremoveFromQueueLocked removeFromFIFOFunc\n\n\t// arrivalR is R(arrivalTime). R is also called \"virtual time\".\n\t// This field is meaningful only while the request is waiting in the virtual world.\n\tarrivalR fcrequest.SeatSeconds\n\n\t// startTime is the real time when the request began executing\n\tstartTime time.Time\n\n\t// Indicates whether client has called Request::Wait()\n\twaitStarted bool\n}\n\ntype completedWorkEstimate struct {\n\tfcrequest.WorkEstimate\n\ttotalWork fcrequest.SeatSeconds // initial plus final work\n\tfinalWork fcrequest.SeatSeconds // only final work\n}\n\n// queue is a sequence of requests that have arrived but not yet finished\n// execution in both the real and virtual worlds\ntype queue struct {\n\t// The requestsWaiting not yet executing in the real world are stored in a FIFO list\n\trequestsWaiting fifo\n\n\t// nextDispatchR is the R progress meter reading at\n\t// which the next request will be dispatched in the virtual world\n\tnextDispatchR fcrequest.SeatSeconds\n\n\t// requestsExecuting is the set of requests executing in the real world\n\trequestsExecuting sets.Set[*request]\n\n\t// index is the position of this queue among those in its queueSet\n\tindex int\n\n\t// seatsInUse is the total number of \"seats\" currently occupied\n\t// by all the requests that are currently executing in this queue\n\tseatsInUse int\n}\n\n// queueSum tracks the sum of initial seats, max seats, and\n// totalWork from all requests in a given queue\ntype queueSum struct {\n\tInitialSeatsSum int\n\tMaxSeatsSum int\n\tTotalWorkSum fcrequest.SeatSeconds\n}\n\nfunc (qs *queueSet) completeWorkEstimate(we *fcrequest.WorkEstimate) completedWorkEstimate {\n\tfinalWork := qs.computeFinalWork(we)\n\treturn completedWorkEstimate{\n\t\tWorkEstimate: *we,\n\t\ttotalWork:    qs.computeInitialWork(we) + finalWork,\n\t\tfinalWork:    finalWork,\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (qs *queueSet) computeInitialWork(we *fcrequest.WorkEstimate) fcrequest.SeatSeconds {\n\treturn fcrequest.SeatsTimesDuration(float64(we.InitialSeats), qs.estimatedServiceDuration)\n}\n\nfunc (qs *queueSet) computeFinalWork(we *fcrequest.WorkEstimate) fcrequest.SeatSeconds {\n\treturn fcrequest.SeatsTimesDuration(float64(we.FinalSeats), we.AdditionalLatency)\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3. **interface.go** - Public API and Configuration\n\n```go\n// QueueSetFactory is used to create QueueSet objects\ntype QueueSetFactory interface {\n\t// BeginConstruction does the first phase of creating a QueueSet\n\t// The RatioedGaugePair observes number of requests,\n\t// execution covering just the regular phase.\n\t// The denominator for the waiting phase is\n\t// max(1, QueuingConfig.QueueLengthLimit) X max(1, QueuingConfig.DesiredNumQueues).\n\t// The RatioedGauge observes number of seats occupied through all phases of execution.\n\t// The denominator for all the ratioed concurrency gauges is supplied later in the DispatchingConfig.\n\t// The Gauge observes the seat demand (executing + queued seats).\n\tBeginConstruction(QueuingConfig, metrics.RatioedGaugePair, metrics.RatioedGauge, metrics.Gauge) (QueueSetCompleter, error)\n}\n\n// QueueSetCompleter finishes the two-step process of creating or reconfiguring a QueueSet\ntype QueueSetCompleter interface {\n\t// Complete returns a QueueSet configured by the given dispatching configuration\n\tComplete(DispatchingConfig) QueueSet\n}\n\n// QueueSet is the abstraction for the queuing and dispatching\n// functionality of one non-exempt priority level\ntype QueueSet interface {\n\t// BeginConfigChange starts the two-step process of updating the configuration\n\t// No change is made until Complete is called. If `C := X.BeginConstruction(q)` \n\t// then `C.Complete(d)` returns the same value `X`. If the QueuingConfig's \n\t// DesiredNumQueues field is zero then the other queuing-specific config parameters \n\t// are not changed, so that the queues continue draining as before.\n\t// In any case, reconfiguration does not discard any queue unless\n\t// and until it is undesired and empty.\n\tBeginConfigChange(QueuingConfig) (QueueSetCompleter, error)\n\n\t// IsIdle returns a bool indicating whether the QueueSet was idle\n\t// at the moment of the return. Idle means the QueueSet has zero\n\t// requests queued and zero executing. This bit can change only\n\t// (1) during a call to StartRequest and (2) during a call to\n\t// Request::Finish. In the latter case idleness can only change\n\t// from false to true.\n\tIsIdle() bool\n\n\t// StartRequest begins the process of handling a request. If the\n\t// request gets queued and the number of queues is greater than 1\n\t// then StartRequest uses the given hashValue as the source of\n\t// entropy as it shuffle-shards the request into a queue. The\n\t// descr1 and descr2 values play no role in the logic but appear\n\t// in log messages. This method always returns quickly (without\n\t// waiting for the request to be dequeued). If this method\n\t// returns a nil Request value then caller should reject the\n\t// request and the returned bool indicates whether the QueueSet\n\t// was idle at the moment of the return. Otherwise idle==false\n\t// and the client must call the Finish method of the Request\n\t// exactly once.\n\tStartRequest(ctx context.Context, width *request.WorkEstimate, hashValue uint64, \n\t\tflowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}, queueNoteFn QueueNoteFn) (req Request, idle bool)\n\n\t// Dump saves and returns the instant internal state of the queue-set.\n\t// Note that dumping process will stop the queue-set from proceeding\n\t// any requests.\n\t// For debugging only.\n\tDump(includeRequestDetails bool) debug.QueueSetDump\n}\n\n// QueueNoteFn is called when a request enters and leaves a queue\ntype QueueNoteFn func(inQueue bool)\n\n// Request represents the remainder of the handling of one request\ntype Request interface {\n\t// Finish determines whether to execute or reject the request and\n\t// invokes `execute` if the decision is to execute the request.\n\t// The returned `idle bool` value indicates whether the QueueSet\n\t// was idle when the value was calculated, but might no longer be\n\t// accurate by the time the client examines that value.\n\tFinish(execute func()) (idle bool)\n}\n\n// QueuingConfig defines the configuration of the queuing aspect of a QueueSet\ntype QueuingConfig struct {\n\t// Name is used to identify a queue set\n\tName string\n\n\t// DesiredNumQueues is the number of queues that should exist now\n\t// This may be non-positive, in which case QueueLengthLimit and HandSize are ignored.\n\t// A value of zero means to respect the ConcurrencyLimit of the DispatchingConfig.\n\t// A negative value means to always dispatch immediately upon arrival\n\t// (i.e., the requests are \"exempt\" from limitation).\n\tDesiredNumQueues int\n\n\t// QueueLengthLimit is the maximum number of requests that may be waiting in a given queue at a time\n\tQueueLengthLimit int\n\n\t// HandSize is a parameter of shuffle sharding. Upon arrival of a request, a queue is chosen by\n\t// randomly dealing a \"hand\" of this many queues and then picking one of minimum length.\n\tHandSize int\n}\n\n// DispatchingConfig defines the configuration of the dispatching aspect of a QueueSet\ntype DispatchingConfig struct {\n\t// ConcurrencyLimit is the maximum number of requests of this QueueSet that may be executing at a time\n\tConcurrencyLimit int\n\n\t// ConcurrencyDenominator is used in relative metrics of concurrency.\n\t// It equals ConcurrencyLimit except when that is zero.\n\tConcurrencyDenominator int\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### 4. **apf_controller.go** - Configuration and Borrowing Management\n\n#### Main Controller Structure:\n\n```go\nconst (\n\t// Borrowing among priority levels is accomplished period\n\tseatDemandIntegrator fq.Integrator\n\n\t// Gauge of seat demand / nominalCL\n\tseatDemandRatioedGauge metrics.RatioedGauge\n\n\t// seatDemandStats is derived from periodically examining the amount\n\tminCL int\n\n\t// maxCL is the nominal limit plus the amount that may be borrowed\n\tmaxCL int\n\n\t// currentCL is the dynamically derived concurrency limit to impose for now\n\tcurrentCL int\n}\n\ntype seatDemandStats struct {\n\tavg           float64\n\tstdDev        float64\n\thighWatermark int\n\tsmoothed      float64\n}\n\nfunc (stats *seatDemandStats) update(obs fq.IntegratorResults) {\n\tstats.highWatermark = int(math.Round(obs.Max))\n\tif obs.Duration <= 0 {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tif math.IsNaN(obs.Deviation) {\n\t\tobs.Deviation = 0\n\t}\n\tstats.avg = obs.Average\n\tstats.stdDev = obs.Deviation\n\tenvelope := obs.Average + obs.Deviation\n\tstats.smoothed = math.Max(envelope, seatDemandSmoothingCoefficient*stats.smoothed+(1-seatDemandSmoothingCoefficient)*envelope)\n}\n```\n\n#### Borrowing Algorithm (updateBorrowingLocked):\n\n```go\nfunc (cfgCtlr *configController) updateBorrowing() {\n\tcfgCtlr.lock.Lock()\n\tdefer cfgCtlr.lock.Unlock()\n\tcfgCtlr.updateBorrowingLocked(true, cfgCtlr.priorityLevelStates)\n}\n\nfunc (cfgCtlr *configController) updateBorrowingLocked(setCompleters bool, \n\tplStates map[string]*priorityLevelState) {\n\titems := make([]allocProblemItem, 0, len(plStates))\n\tnonExemptPLNames := make([]string, 0, len(plStates))\n\tidxOfNonExempt := map[string]int{}  // items index of non-exempt classes\n\tcclOfExempt := map[string]int{}     // minCurrentCL of exempt classes\n\tvar minCLSum, minCurrentCLSum int   // sums over non-exempt classes\n\tremainingServerCL := cfgCtlr.nominalCLSum\n\t\n\tfor plName, plState := range plStates {\n\t\tobs := plState.seatDemandIntegrator.Reset()\n\t\tplState.seatDemandStats.update(obs)\n\t\tvar minCurrentCL int\n\t\t\n\t\tif plState.pl.Spec.Type == flowcontrol.PriorityLevelEnablementExempt {\n\t\t\tminCurrentCL = max(plState.minCL, plState.seatDemandStats.highWatermark)\n\t\t\tcclOfExempt[plName] = minCurrentCL\n\t\t\tremainingServerCL -= minCurrentCL\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// Lower bound on this priority level's adjusted concurrency limit is the lesser of:\n\t\t\t// - its seat demand high watermark over the last adjustment period, and\n\t\t\t// - its configured concurrency limit.\n\t\t\t// BUT: we do not want this to be lower than the lower bound from configuration.\n\t\t\tminCurrentCL = max(plState.minCL, min(plState.nominalCL, plState.seatDemandStats.highWatermark))\n\t\t\tidxOfNonExempt[plName] = len(items)\n\t\t\tnonExemptPLNames = append(nonExemptPLNames, plName)\n\t\t\titems = append(items, allocProblemItem{\n\t\t\t\tlowerBound: float64(minCurrentCL),\n\t\t\t\tupperBound: float64(plState.maxCL),\n\t\t\t\ttarget:     math.Max(float64(minCurrentCL), plState.seatDemandStats.smoothed),\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t\tminCLSum += plState.minCL\n\t\t\tminCurrentCLSum += minCurrentCL\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\t\n\tif len(items) == 0 && cfgCtlr.nominalCLSum > 0 {\n\t\tklog.ErrorS(nil, \"Impossible: no priority levels\", \"plStates\", cfgCtlr.priorityLevelStates)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\t\n\tvar allocs []float64\n\tvar shareFrac, fairFrac float64\n\tvar err error\n\t\n\tif remainingServerCL <= minCLSum {\n\t\tmetrics.SetFairFrac(0)\n\t} else if remainingServerCL <= minCurrentCLSum {\n\t\tshareFrac = float64(remainingServerCL-minCLSum) / float64(minCurrentCLSum-minCLSum)\n\t\tmetrics.SetFairFrac(0)\n\t} else {\n\t\tallocs, fairFrac, err = computeConcurrencyAllocation(cfgCtlr.nominalCLSum, items)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(err, \"Unable to derive new concurrency limits\", \n\t\t\t\t\"plNames\", nonExemptPLNames, \"items\", items)\n\t\t\tallocs = make([]float64, len(items))\n\t\t\tfor idx, plName := range nonExemptPLNames {\n\t\t\t\tplState := plStates[plName]\n\t\t\t\tallocs[idx] = float64(plState.currentCL)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tmetrics.SetFairFrac(float64(fairFrac))\n\t}\n\t\n\tfor plName, plState := range plStates {\n\t\tidx, isNonExempt := idxOfNonExempt[plName]\n\t\tif setCompleters {\n\t\t\tqsCompleter, err := queueSetCompleterForPL(cfgCtlr.queueSetFactory, plState.queues,\n\t\t\t\tplState.pl, plState.reqsGaugePair, plState.execSeatsObs,\n\t\t\t\tmetrics.NewUnionGauge(plState.seatDemandIntegrator, plState.seatDemandRatioedGauge))\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(err, \"Inconceivable!  Configuration error in existing priority level\", \"pl\", plState.pl)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tplState.qsCompleter = qsCompleter\n\t\t}\n\t\tvar currentCL int\n\t\tif !isNonExempt {\n\t\t\tcurrentCL = cclOfExempt[plName]\n\t\t} else if remainingServerCL <= minCLSum {\n\t\t\tcurrentCL = plState.minCL\n\t\t} else if remainingServerCL <= minCurrentCLSum {\n\t\t\tminCurrentCL := max(plState.minCL, min(plState.nominalCL, plState.seatDemandStats.highWatermark))\n\t\t\tcurrentCL = plState.minCL + int(math.Round(float64(minCurrentCL-plState.minCL)*shareFrac))\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tcurrentCL = int(math.Round(float64(allocs[idx])))\n\t\t}\n\t\t\n\t\trelChange := relDiff(float64(currentCL), float64(plState.currentCL))\n\t\tplState.currentCL = currentCL\n\t\tmetrics.NotePriorityLevelConcurrencyAdjustment(plState.pl.Name, \n\t\t\tfloat64(plState.seatDemandStats.highWatermark), plState.seatDemandStats.avg, \n\t\t\tplState.seatDemandStats.stdDev, plState.seatDemandStats.smoothed, \n\t\t\tfloat64(items[idx].target), currentCL)\n\t\t\n\t\tlogLevel := klog.Level(4)\n\t\tif relChange >= 0.05 {\n\t\t\tlogLevel = 2\n\t\t}\n\t\tvar concurrencyDenominator int\n\t\tif currentCL > 0 {\n\t\t\tconcurrencyDenominator = currentCL\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tconcurrencyDenominator = int(math.Max(1, math.Round(float64(cfgCtlr.serverConcurrencyLimit)/10)))\n\t\t}\n\t\tplState.seatDemandRatioedGauge.SetDenominator(float64(concurrencyDenominator))\n\t\tklog.V(logLevel).InfoS(\"Update CurrentCL\", \"plName\", plName, \n\t\t\t\"seatDemandHighWatermark\", plState.seatDemandStats.highWatermark, \n\t\t\t\"seatDemandAvg\", plState.seatDemandStats.avg, \n\t\t\t\"seatDemandStdev\", plState.seatDemandStats.stdDev, \n\t\t\t\"seatDemandSmoothed\", plState.seatDemandStats.smoothed, \n\t\t\t\"fairFrac\", fairFrac, \"currentCL\", currentCL, \n\t\t\t\"concurrencyDenominator\", concurrencyDenominator, \"backstop\", err != nil)\n\t\t\n\t\t// Update QueueSet with new concurrency limit\n\t\tplState.queues = plState.qsCompleter.Complete(fq.DispatchingConfig{\n\t\t\tConcurrencyLimit: currentCL, \n\t\t\tConcurrencyDenominator: concurrencyDenominator,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary of Key Concepts\n\n### **Virtual Time (R meter)**\n- Advances based on active queue demand and concurrency limit\n- Rate: `min(seatsRequested, concurrencyLimit) / activeQueues`\n- Overflow prevention via epoch advancement (subtracts rDecrement every time R > highR)\n\n### **Fair Queuing Algorithm**\n- Uses virtual finish time: `queue.nextDispatchR + request.totalWork()`\n- Selects queue with minimum virtual finish time (round-robin among tied queues)\n- Updates `nextDispatchR` after dispatch: `nextDispatchR += request.totalWork()`\n\n### **Borrowing Mechanism**\n- Periodic adjustment every 10 seconds\n- Tracks seat demand statistics (average, std dev, high watermark, smoothed)\n- Allocates concurrency limits between priority levels based on observed demand\n- Exempt priority levels get precedence; remaining capacity distributed fairly\n\n### **Anti-Windup**\n- Prevents queues from advancing ahead of arrivals\n- Bounds `nextDispatchR \u2265 arrivalR` of oldest waiting request\n- Applied whenever queue state changes\n\n### **Work Estimation**\n- Initial work: `InitialSeats * estimatedServiceDuration`\n- Final work: `FinalSeats * AdditionalLatency`\n- Total work is sum of initial and final work\n\nThis comprehensive implementation ensures fair allocation of API server concurrency across priority levels while supporting dynamic borrowing based on actual demand.",

The fields listed before the lock\\n71: // should not be changed; the fields listed after the\\n72: // lock must be accessed only while holding the lock.\\n73: //\\n74: // The methods of this type follow the naming convention that the\\n75: // suffix \\\"Locked\\\" means the caller must hold the lock; for a method\\n76: // whose name does not end in \\\"Locked\\\" either acquires the lock or\\n77: // does not care about locking.\\n78: //\\n79: // The methods of this type also follow the convention that the suffix\\n80: // \\\"ToBoundLocked\\\" means that the caller may have to follow up with a\\n81: // call to `boundNextDispatchLocked`. Its\\n100: \\t// DesiredNumQueues may be less than the current number of queues.\\n101: \\t// If its DesiredNumQueues is zero then its other queuing\\n102: \\t// parameters retain the settings they had when DesiredNumQueues\\n103: \\t// was last non-zero (if ever).\\n104: \\tqCfg fq.QueuingConfig\\n105: \\n106: \\t// the current dispatching configuration.\\n107: \\tdCfg fq.DispatchingConfig\\n108: \\n109: \\t// If `qCfg.DesiredNumQueues` is non-zero then dealer is not nil\\n110: \\t// and is good for `qCfg`.\\n111: \\tdealer *shufflesharding.Dealer\\n112: \\n113: \\t// queues may be longer than the desired number, while the excess\\n114: \\t// queues are still draining.\\n115: \\tqueues []*queue\\n116: \\n117: \\t// currentR is the amount of seat-seconds allocated per queue since process startup.\\n118: \\t// This is our generalization of the progress meter named R in the original fair queuing work.\\n119: \\tcurrentR fqrequest.SeatSeconds\\n120: \\n121: \\t// lastRealTime is what `clock.Now()` yielded when `virtualTime` was last updated\\n122: \\tlastRealTime time.Time\\n123: \\n124: \\t// robinIndex is the index of the last queue dispatched\\n125: \\trobinIndex int\\n126: \\n127: \\t// totRequestsWaiting is the sum, over all the queues, of the\\n128: \\t// number of requests waiting in that queue\\n129: \\ttotRequestsWaiting int\\n130: \\n131: \\t// totRequestsExecuting is the total number of requests of this\\n132: \\t// queueSet that are currently executing.  That is the same as the\\n133: \\t// sum, over all the queues, of the number of requests executing\\n134: \\t// from that queue.\\n135: \\ttotRequestsExecuting int\\n136: \\n137: \\t// \\ttotSeatsInUse int\\n144: \\n145: \\t// totSeatsWaiting is the sum, over all the waiting requests, of their\\n146: \\t// max width.\\n147: \\ttotSeatsWaiting int\\n148: \\n149: \\t// enqueues is the number of requests that have ever been enqueued\\n150: \\tenqueues int\\n151: \\n152: \\t// totRequestsDispatched is the total number of requests of this\\n153: \\t// queueSet that have been processed.\\n154: \\ttotRequestsDispatched int\\n155: \\n156: \\t// totRequestsRejected is the total number of requests of this\\n157: \\t// queueSet that have been rejected.\\n158: \\ttotRequestsRejected int\\n159: \\n160: \\t// totRequestsTimedout is the total number of requests of this\\n161: \\t// queueSet that have been timeouted.\\n162: \\ttotRequestsTimedout int\\n163: \\n164: \\t// totRequestsCancelled is the total number of requests of this\\n165: \\t// queueSet that have been cancelled.\\n166: \\ttotRequestsCancelled int\\n167: }\\n168: \\n169: // ordinaryPromiseFactoryFactory)\\n172: }\\n173: \\n174: // newTestableQueueSetFactory creates a new QueueSetFactory object with the given promiseFactoryFactory\\n175: func newTestableQueueSetFactory(c fq.QueueNoteFn) (fq.Request, bool) {\\n309: \\tqs.lockAndSyncTime(ctx)\\n310: \\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\\n311: \\tvar req *request\\n312: \\n313: \\t// Thus, it should be invoked after acquiring the\\n464: // lock and before modifying the state of any queue.\\n465: func (qs *queueSet) syncTimeLocked(ctx context.Context) {\\n466: \\trealNow := fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds / 2\\n484: \\n485: // highR is the threshold that triggers advance of the epoch.\\n486: // That is, decrementing the global progress meter R by rDecrement.\\n487: const highR = rDecrement + rDecrement/2\\n488: \\n489: // advanceEpoch subtracts rDecrement from the global progress meter R\\n490: // and all the readings that have been taked from that meter.\\n491: // The now and incrR parameters are only used to add info to the log messages.\\n492: func (qs *queueSet) advanceEpoch(ctx context.Context, now time.Time, incrR fqrequest.SeatSeconds) {\\n493: \\toldR := qs.currentR\\n494: \\tqs.currentR -= rDecrement\\n495: \\tklog.InfoS(\\\"Advancing epoch\\\", \\\"QS\\\", qs.qCfg.Name, \\\"when\\\", now.Format(nsTimeFmt), \\\"oldR\\\", oldR, \\\"newR\\\", qs.currentR, \\\"incrR\\\", incrR)\\n496: \\tsuccess := true\\n497: \\tfor qIdx, queue := range qs.queues {\\n498: \\t\\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() == 0 && queue.requestsExecuting.Len() == 0 }\\n523: \\n524: // getVirtualTimeRatio calculates the rate at which virtual time has\\n525: // been advancing, according to the logic in `doc.go`.\\n526: func (qs *queueSet) getVirtualTimeRatioLocked() float64 {\\n527: \\tactiveQueues := 0\\n528: \\tseatsRequested := 0\\n529: \\tfor _, queue := range qs.queues {\\n530: \\t\\t// here we want the sum of the maximum width of the requests in this queue since our\\n531: \\t\\t// goal is to find the maximum rate at which the queue could work.\\n532: \\t\\tseatsRequested += (queue.seatsInUse + queue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum().MaxSeatsSum)\\n533: \\t\\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() > 0 || queue.requestsExecuting.Len() > 0 {\\n534: \\t\\t\\tactiveQueues++\\n535: \\t\\t}\\n536: \\t}\\n537: \\tif activeQueues == 0 {\\n538: \\t\\treturn 0\\n539: \\t}\\n540: \\treturn math.Min(float64(seatsRequested), float64(qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)) / float64(activeQueues)\\n541: }\\n542: \\n543: // shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked encapsulates the logic required\\n544: // to validate and enqueue a request for the queueSet/QueueSet:\\n545: // 1) Start with shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\\n546: // 2) Reject current request if there is not enough concurrency shares and\\n547: // we are at max queue length\\n548: // 3) If not rejected, create a request and enqueue\\n549: // The fields listed before the lock\n71: // should not be changed; the fields listed after the\n72: // lock must be accessed only while holding the lock.\n73: //\n74: // The methods of this type follow the naming convention that the\n75: // suffix \"Locked\" means the caller must hold the lock; for a method\n76: // whose name does not end in \"Locked\" either acquires the lock or\n77: // does not care about locking.\n78: //\n79: // The methods of this type also follow the convention that the suffix\n80: // \"ToBoundLocked\" means that the caller may have to follow up with a\n81: // call to `boundNextDispatchLocked`.  This is so for a method that\n82: // changes what request is oldest in a queue, because that change means\n83: // that the anti-windup hack in boundNextDispatchLocked needs to be\n84: // applied wrt the revised oldest request in the queue.\n85: type queueSet struct {\n86: \tclock                    eventclock.Interface\n87: \testimatedServiceDuration time.Duration\n88: \n89: \treqsGaugePair metrics.RatioedGaugePair // .RequestsExecuting covers regular phase only\n90: \n91: \texecSeatsGauge metrics.RatioedGauge // for all phases of execution\n92: \n93: \tseatDemandIntegrator metrics.Gauge\n94: \n95: \tpromiseFactory promiseFactory\n96: \n97: \tlock sync.Mutex\n98: \n99: \t// qCfg holds the current queuing configuration.  Its\n100: \t// DesiredNumQueues may be less than the current number of queues.\n101: \t// If its DesiredNumQueues is zero then its other queuing\n102: \t// parameters retain the settings they had when DesiredNumQueues\n103: \t// was last non-zero (if ever).\n104: \tqCfg fq.QueuingConfig\n105: \n106: \t// the current dispatching configuration.\n107: \tdCfg fq.DispatchingConfig\n108: \n109: \t// If `qCfg.DesiredNumQueues` is non-zero then dealer is not nil\n110: \t// and is good for `qCfg`.\n111: \tdealer *shufflesharding.Dealer\n112: \n113: \t// queues may be longer than the desired number, while the excess\n114: \t// queues are still draining.\n115: \tqueues []*queue\n116: \n117: \t// currentR is the amount of seat-seconds allocated per queue since process startup.\n118: \t// This is our generalization of the progress meter named R in the original fair queuing work.\n119: \tcurrentR fqrequest.SeatSeconds\n120: \n121: \t// lastRealTime is what `clock.Now()` yielded when `virtualTime` was last updated\n122: \tlastRealTime time.Time\n123: \n124: \t// robinIndex is the index of the last queue dispatched\n125: \trobinIndex int\n126: \n127: \t// totRequestsWaiting is the sum, over all the queues, of the\n128: \t// number of requests waiting in that queue\n129: \ttotRequestsWaiting int\n130: \n131: \t// totRequestsExecuting is the total number of requests of this\n132: \t// queueSet that are currently executing. \tqs.dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked()\n287: }\n288: \n289: // A decision about a request\n290: type requestDecision int\n291: \n292: // Values passed through a request's decision\n293: const (\n294: \t// Serve this one\n295: \tdecisionExecute requestDecision = iota\n296: \n297: \t// This one's context timed out / was canceled\n298: \tdecisionCancel\n299: )\n300: \n301: // StartRequest begins the process of handling a request.  We take the\n302: // approach of updating the metrics about total requests queued and\n303: // executing at each point where there is a change in that quantity,\n304: // because the metrics --- and only the metrics --- track that\n305: // quantity per FlowSchema.\n306: // The queueSet's promiseFactory is invoked once if the returned Request is non-nil,\n307: // not invoked if the Request is nil.\n308: func (qs *queueSet) StartRequest(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, hashValue uint64, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}, queueNoteFn fq.QueueNoteFn) (fq.Request, bool) {\n309: \tqs.lockAndSyncTime(ctx)\n310: \tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n311: \tvar req *request\n312: \n313: \t// ========================================================================\n314: \t// Step 0:\n315: \t// Apply only concurrency limit, if zero queues desired\n316: \tif qs.qCfg.DesiredNumQueues < 1 {\n317: \t\tif !qs.canAccommodateSeatsLocked(workEstimate.MaxSeats()) {\n318: \t\t\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): rejecting request %q %#+v %#+v because %d seats are asked for, %d seats are in use (%d are \t\t\tqs.totRequestsRejected++\n321: \t\t\tmetrics.AddReject(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, \"concurrency-limit\")\n322: \t\t\treturn nil, qs.isIdleLocked()\n323: \t\t}\n324: \t\treq = qs.dispatchSansQueueLocked(ctx, workEstimate, flowDistinguisher, fsName, descr1, descr2)\n325: \t\treturn req, false\n326: \t}\n327: \n328: \t// ========================================================================\n329: \t// Step 1:\n330: \t// 1) Start with shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n331: \t// 2) Reject current request if there is not enough concurrency shares and\n332: \t// we are at max queue length\n333: \t// 3) If not rejected, create a request and enqueue\n334: \treq = qs.shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked(ctx, \t\tqs.totRequestsRejected++\n340: \t\tmetrics.AddReject(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, \"queue-full\")\n341: \t\treturn nil, qs.isIdleLocked()\n342: \t}\n343: \n344: \t// ========================================================================\n345: \t// Step 2:\n346: \t// The next step is to invoke the method that dequeues as much\n347: \t// as possible.\n348: \t// This method runs a loop, as long as there are non-empty\n349: \t// queues and the number currently executing is less than the\n350: \t// assured concurrency value.  The body of the loop uses the\n351: \t// fair queuing technique to pick a queue and dispatch a\n352: \t// request from that queue.\n353: \tqs.dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked()\n354: \n355: \treturn req, false\n356: }\n357: \n358: // ordinaryPromiseFactoryFactory is the promiseFactoryFactory that\n359: // a queueSetFactory would ordinarily use.\n360: // Test code might use something different.\n361: func ordinaryPromiseFactoryFactory(qs *queueSet) promiseFactory {\n362: \treturn promise.NewWriteOnce\n363: }\n364: \n365: // MaxSeats returns the maximum number of seats this request requires, it is\n366: // the maxumum of the two - WorkEstimate.InitialSeats, WorkEstimate.FinalSeats.\n367: func (req *request) MaxSeats() int {\n368: \treturn req.workEstimate.MaxSeats()\n369: }\n370: \n371: func (req *request) InitialSeats() int {\n372: \treturn int(req.workEstimate.InitialSeats)\n373: }\n374: \n375: func (req *request) NoteQueued(inQueue bool) {\n376: \tif req.queueNoteFn != nil {\n377: \t\treq.queueNoteFn(inQueue)\n378: \t}\n379: }\n380: \n381: func (req *request) Finish(execFn func()) bool {\n382: \texec, idle := req.wait()\n383: \tif !exec {\n384: \t\treturn idle\n385: \t}\n386: \tfunc() {\n387: \t\tdefer func() {\n388: \t\t\tidle = req.qs.finishRequestAndDispatchAsMuchAsPossible(req)\n389: \t\t}()\n390: \n391: \t\texecFn()\n392: \t}()\n393: \n394: \treturn idle\n395: }\n396: \n397: func (req *request) wait() (bool, bool) {\n398: \tqs := req.qs\n399: \n400: \t// ========================================================================\n401: \t// Step 3:\n402: \t// The final step is to wait on a decision from\n403: \t// somewhere and then act on it.\n404: \tdecisionAny := req.decision.Get()\n405: \tqs.lockAndSyncTime(req.ctx)\n406: \tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n407: \tif req.waitStarted {\n408: \t\t// This can not happen, because the client is forbidden to\n409: \t\t// call Wait twice on the same request\n410: \t\tklog.Errorf(\"Duplicate call to the Wait method!  Immediately returning execute=false.  QueueSet=%s, startTime=%s, descr1=%#+v, descr2=%#+v\", req.qs.qCfg.Name, req.startTime, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n411: \t\treturn false, qs.isIdleLocked()\n412: \t}\n413: \treq.waitStarted = true\n414: \tswitch decisionAny {\n415: \tcase decisionCancel: // handle in code following this switch\n416: \tcase decisionExecute:\n417: \t\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): Dispatching request %#+v %#+v from its queue\", qs.qCfg.Name, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n418: \t\treturn true, false\n419: \tdefault:\n420: \t\t// This can not happen, all possible values are handled above\n421: \t\tklog.Errorf(\"QS(%s): Impossible decision (type %T, value %#+v) for request %#+v %#+v!  Treating as cancel\", qs.qCfg.Name, decisionAny, decisionAny, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n422: \t}\n423: \t// TODO(aaron-prindle) add metrics for this case\n424: \tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): Ejecting request %#+v %#+v from its queue\", qs.qCfg.Name, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n425: \t// remove the request from the queue as its queue wait time has exceeded\n426: \tqueue := req.queue\n427: \tif req.removeFromQueueLocked() != nil {\n428: \t\tdefer qs.boundNextDispatchLocked(queue)\n429: \t\tqs.totRequestsWaiting--\n430: \t\tqs.totSeatsWaiting -= req.MaxSeats()\n431: \t\tqs.totRequestsRejected++\n432: \t\tqs.totRequestsCancelled++\n433: \t\tmetrics.AddReject(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, \"time-out\")\n434: \t\tmetrics.AddRequestsInQueues(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, -1)\n435: \t\tmetrics.AddSeatsInQueues(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, -req.MaxSeats())\n436: \t\treq.NoteQueued(false)\n437: \t\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsWaiting.Add(-1)\n438: \t\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n439: \t}\n440: \treturn false, qs.isIdleLocked()\n441: }\n442: \n443: func (qs *queueSet) IsIdle() bool {\n444: \tqs.lock.Lock()\n445: \tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n446: \treturn qs.isIdleLocked()\n447: }\n448: \n449: func (qs *queueSet) isIdleLocked() bool {\n450: \treturn qs.totRequestsWaiting == 0 && qs.totRequestsExecuting == 0\n451: }\n452: \n453: // lockAndSyncTime acquires the lock and updates the virtual time.\n454: // Doing them together avoids the mistake of modifying some queue state\n455: // before calling syncTimeLocked.\n456: func (qs *queueSet) lockAndSyncTime(ctx context.Context) {\n457: \tqs.lock.Lock()\n458: \tqs.syncTimeLocked(ctx)\n459: }\n460: \n461: // syncTimeLocked updates the virtual time based on the assumption\n462: // that the current state of the queues has been in effect since\n463: // `qs.lastRealTime`.  Thus, it should be invoked after acquiring the\n464: // lock and before modifying the state of any queue.\n465: func (qs *queueSet) syncTimeLocked(ctx context.Context) {\n466: \trealNow := qs.clock.Now()\n467: \ttimeSinceLast := realNow.Sub(qs.lastRealTime)\n468: \tqs.lastRealTime = realNow\n469: \tprevR := qs.currentR\n470: \tincrR := fqrequest.SeatsTimesDuration(qs.getVirtualTimeRatioLocked(), timeSinceLast)\n471: \tqs.currentR = prevR + incrR\n472: \tswitch {\n473: \tcase prevR > qs.currentR:\n474: \t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"queueset::currentR overflow\"), \"Overflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"when\", realNow.Format(nsTimeFmt), \"prevR\", prevR, \"incrR\", incrR, \"currentR\", qs.currentR)\n475: \tcase qs.currentR >= highR:\n476: \t\tqs.advanceEpoch(ctx, realNow, incrR)\n477: \t}\n478: \tmetrics.SetCurrentR(qs.qCfg.Name, qs.currentR.ToFloat())\n479: }\n480: \n481: // rDecrement is the amount by which the progress meter R is wound backwards\n482: // when needed to avoid overflow.\n483: const rDecrement = fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds / 2\n484: \n485: // highR is the threshold that triggers advance of the epoch.\n486: // That is, decrementing the global progress meter R by rDecrement.\n487: const highR = rDecrement + rDecrement/2\n488: \n489: // advanceEpoch subtracts rDecrement from the global progress meter R\n490: // and all the readings that have been taked from that meter.\n491: // The now and incrR parameters are only used to add info to the log messages.\n492: func (qs *queueSet) advanceEpoch(ctx context.Context, now time.Time, incrR fqrequest.SeatSeconds) {\n493: \toldR := qs.currentR\n494: \tqs.currentR -= rDecrement\n495: \tklog.InfoS(\"Advancing epoch\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"when\", now.Format(nsTimeFmt), \"oldR\", oldR, \"newR\", qs.currentR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n496: \tsuccess := true\n497: \tfor qIdx, queue := range qs.queues {\n498: \t\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() == 0 && queue.requestsExecuting.Len() == 0 {\n499: \t\t\t// Do not just decrement, the value could be quite outdated.\n500: \t\t\t// It is safe to reset to zero in this case, because the next request\n501: \t\t\t// will overwrite the zero with `qs.currentR`.\n502: \t\t\tqueue.nextDispatchR = 0\n503: \t\t\tcontinue\n504: \t\t}\n505: \t\toldNextDispatchR := queue.nextDispatchR\n506: \t\tqueue.nextDispatchR -= rDecrement\n507: \t\tif queue.nextDispatchR > oldNextDispatchR {\n508: \t\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"queue::nextDispatchR underflow\"), \"Underflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"queue\", qIdx, \"oldNextDispatchR\", oldNextDispatchR, \"newNextDispatchR\", queue.nextDispatchR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n509: \t\t\tsuccess = false\n510: \t\t}\n511: \t\tqueue.requestsWaiting.Walk(func(req *request) bool {\n512: \t\t\toldArrivalR := req.arrivalR\n513: \t\t\treq.arrivalR -= rDecrement\n514: \t\t\tif req.arrivalR > oldArrivalR {\n515: \t\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"request::arrivalR underflow\"), \"Underflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"queue\", qIdx, \"request\", *req, \"oldArrivalR\", oldArrivalR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n516: \t\t\t\tsuccess = false\n517: \t\t\t}\n518: \t\t\treturn true\n519: \t\t})\n520: \t}\n521: \tmetrics.AddEpochAdvance(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, success)\n522: }\n523: \n524: // getVirtualTimeRatio calculates the rate at which virtual time has\n525: // been advancing, according to the logic in `doc.go`.\n526: func (qs *queueSet) getVirtualTimeRatioLocked() float64 {\n527: \tactiveQueues := 0\n528: \tseatsRequested := 0\n529: \tfor _, queue := range qs.queues {\n530: \t\t// here we want the sum of the maximum width of the requests in this queue since our\n531: \t\t// goal is to find the maximum rate at which the queue could work.\n532: \t\tseatsRequested += (queue.seatsInUse + queue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum().MaxSeatsSum)\n533: \t\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() > 0 || queue.requestsExecuting.Len() > 0 {\n534: \t\t\tactiveQueues++\n535: \t\t}\n536: \t}\n537: \tif activeQueues == 0 {\n538: \t\treturn 0\n539: \t}\n540: \treturn math.Min(float64(seatsRequested), float64(qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)) / float64(activeQueues)\n541: }\n542: \n543: // shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked encapsulates the logic required\n544: // to validate and enqueue a request for the queueSet/QueueSet:\n545: // 1) Start with shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n546: // 2) Reject current request if there is not enough concurrency shares and\n547: // we are at max queue length\n548: // 3) If not rejected, create a request and enqueue\n549: // returns the enqueud request on a successful enqueue\n550: // returns nil in the case that there is no available concurrency or\n551: // the queuelengthlimit has been reached\n552: func (qs *queueSet) shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, hashValue uint64, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}, queueNoteFn fq.QueueNoteFn) *request {\n553: \t// Start with the shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n554: \tqueueIdx := qs.shuffleShardLocked(hashValue, descr1, descr2)\n555: \tqueue := qs.queues[queueIdx]\n556: \n557: \tdefer qs.boundNextDispatchLocked(queue)\n558: \n559: \t// Create a ctx,\n565: \t\tdecision:          qs.promiseFactory(nil, ctx, decisionCancel),\n566: \t\tarrivalTime:       qs.clock.Now(),\n567: \t\tarrivalR:          qs.currentR,\n568: \t\tqueue: \t}\n574: \tif ok := qs.rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked(req); !ok {\n575: \t\treturn nil\n576: \t}\n577: \tmetrics.ObserveQueueLength(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, queue.requestsWaiting.Length())\n578: \treturn req\n579: }\n580: \n581: // shuffleShardLocked uses shuffle sharding to select a queue index\n582: // using the given hashValue and the shuffle sharding parameters of the queueSet.\n583: func (qs *queueSet) shuffleShardLocked(hashValue uint64, descr1, descr2 interface{}) int {\n584: \tvar backHand [8]int\n585: \t// Deal into a data structure, so that the order of visit below is not necessarily the order of the deal.\n586: \t// This removes bias in the case of flows with overlapping hands.\n587: \thand := qs.dealer.DealIntoHand(hashValue, backHand[:])\n588: \thandSize := {\n594: \t\tqueueIdx := hand[(offset+i)%handSize]\n595: \t\tqueue := qs.queues[queueIdx]\n596: \t\tqueueSum := queue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum()\n597: \n598: \t\t// this is the total amount of work in seat-seconds for requests\n599: \t\t// waiting in this queue, we will select the queue with the minimum.\n600: \t\tthisQueueSeatSeconds := queueSum.TotalWorkSum\n601: \t\tklog.V(7).Infof(\"QS(%s): For nextDispatchR=%v\", qs.qCfg.Name, qs.clock.Now().Format(nsTimeFmt), qs.currentR, descr1, descr2, bestQueueIdx, chosenQueue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum(), chosenQueue.seatsInUse, chosenQueue.nextDispatchR)\n610: \t}\n611: \treturn bestQueueIdx\n612: }\n613: \n614: // rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked rejects or enqueues the newly arrived\n615: // request, which has been assigned to a queue.  If up against the\n616: // queue length limit and the concurrency limit then returns false.\n617: // Otherwise enqueues and returns true.\n618: func (qs *queueSet) rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked(request *request) bool {\n619: \tqueue := request.queue\n620: \tcurQueueLength := queue.requestsWaiting.Length()\n621: \t// rejects the newly arrived request if resource criteria not met\n622: \tif dispatchSansQueueLocked(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}) *request {\n660: \t// does not call metrics.SetDispatchMetrics because there is no queuing and thus no interesting virtual world\n661: \tnow := qs.clock.Now()\n662: \treq := &request{\n663: \t\tqs:                qs,\n664: \t\tfsName: canAccommodateSeatsLocked(seats int) bool {\n749: \tswitch {\n750: \tcase qs.qCfg.DesiredNumQueues < 0:\n751: \t\t// This is code for exemption from limitation\n752: \t\treturn true\n753: \tcase seats > qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit:\n754: \t\t// we have picked the queue with the minimum virtual finish time, but\n755: \t\t// the number of seats this request asks for exceeds the concurrency limit.\n756: and also returns that request.\n774: // Returns nils if the head of the selected queue can not be dispatched now,\n775: // in which case the caller does not need to follow up     "content": "1: /*\n2: Copyright 2019 The Kubernetes Authors.\n3: \n4: Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the \"License\");\n5: you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.\n6: You may obtain a copy of the License at\n7: \n8:     http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0\n9: \n10: Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software\n11: distributed under the License is distributed on an \"AS IS\" BASIS,\n12: WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.\n13: See the License for the specific language governing permissions and\n14: limitations under the License.\n15: */\n16: \n17: package fairqueuing\n18: \n19: import (\n20: \t\"context\"\n21: \n22: \t\"k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/debug\"\n23: \t\"k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/metrics\"\n24: \t\"k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/request\"\n25: )\n26: \n27: // QueueSetFactory is used to create QueueSet objects.  Creation, like\n28: // config update, is done in two phases: the first phase consumes the\n29: // QueuingConfig and the second consumes the DispatchingConfig.  They\n30: // are separated so that errors from the first phase can be found\n31: // before committing to a concurrency allotment for the second.\n32: type QueueSetFactory interface {\n33: \t// BeginConstruction does the first phase of creating a QueueSet.\n34: \t// The RatioedGaugePair observes number of requests,\n35: \t// execution covering just the regular phase.\n36: \t// The denominator for the waiting phase is\n37: \t// max(1, QueuingConfig.QueueLengthLimit) X max(1, QueuingConfig.DesiredNumQueues).\n38: \t// The RatioedGauge observes number of seats occupied through all phases of execution.\n39: \t// The denominator for all the ratioed concurrency gauges is supplied later in the DispatchingConfig.\n40: \t// The Gauge observes the seat demand (executing + queued seats).\n41: \tBeginConstruction(QueuingConfig, metrics.RatioedGaugePair, metrics.RatioedGauge, metrics.Gauge) (QueueSetCompleter, error)\n42: }\n43: \n44: // QueueSetCompleter finishes the two-step process of creating or\n45: // reconfiguring a QueueSet\n46: type QueueSetCompleter interface {\n47: \t// Complete returns a QueueSet configured by the given\n48: \t// dispatching configuration.\n49: \tComplete(DispatchingConfig) QueueSet\n50: }\n51: \n52: // QueueSet is the abstraction for the queuing and dispatching\n53: // functionality of one non-exempt priority level.  It covers the\n54: // functionality described in the \"Assignment to a Queue\", \"Queuing\",\n55: // and \"Dispatching\" sections of\n56: // https://github.com/kubernetes/enhancements/blob/master/keps/sig-api-machinery/1040-priority-and-fairness/README.md\n57: // .  Some day we may have connections between priority levels, but\n58: // today is not that day.\n59: type QueueSet interface {\n60: \t// BeginConfigChange starts the two-step process of updating the\n61: \t// configuration.  No change is made until Complete is called.  If\n62: \t// `C := X.BeginConstruction(q)` then `C.Complete(d)` returns the\n63: \t// same value `X`.  If the QueuingConfig's DesiredNumQueues field\n64: \t// is zero then the other queuing-specific config parameters are\n65: \t// not changed, so that the queues continue draining as before.\n66: \t// In any case, reconfiguration does not discard any queue unless\n67: \t// and until it is undesired and empty.\n68: \tBeginConfigChange(QueuingConfig) (QueueSetCompleter, error)\n69: \n70: \t// IsIdle returns a bool indicating whether the QueueSet was idle\n71: \t// at the moment of the return.  Idle means the QueueSet has zero\n72: \t// requests queued and zero executing.  This bit can change only\n73: \t// (1) during a call to StartRequest and (2) during a call to\n74: \t// Request::Finish.  In the latter case idleness can only change\n75: \t// from false to true.\n76: \tIsIdle() bool\n77: \n78: \t// StartRequest begins the process of handling a request.  If the\n79: \t// request gets queued and the number of queues is greater than 1\n80: \t// then StartRequest uses the given hashValue as the source of\n81: \t// entropy as it shuffle-shards the request into a queue.  The\n82: \t// descr1 and descr2 values play no role in the logic but appear\n83: \t// in log messages.  This method always returns quickly (without\n84: \t// waiting for the request to be dequeued).  If this method\n85: \t// returns a nil Request value then caller should reject the\n86: \t// request and the returned bool indicates whether the QueueSet\n87: \t// was idle at the moment of the return.  Otherwise idle==false\n88: \t// and the client must call the Finish method of the Request\n89: \t// exactly once.\n90: \tStartRequest(ctx context.Context, width *request.WorkEstimate, hashValue uint64, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}, queueNoteFn QueueNoteFn) (req Request, idle bool)\n91: \n92: \t// Dump saves and returns the instant internal state of the queue-set.\n93: \t// Note that dumping process will stop the queue-set from proceeding\n94: \t// any requests.\n95: \t// For debugging only.\n96: \tDump(includeRequestDetails bool) debug.QueueSetDump\n97: }\n98: \n99: // QueueNoteFn is called when a request enters and leaves a queue\n100: type QueueNoteFn func(inQueue bool)\n101: \n102: // Request represents the remainder of the handling of one request\n103: type Request interface {\n104: \t// Finish determines whether to execute or reject the request and\n105: \t// invokes `execute` if the decision is to execute the request.\n106: \t// The returned `idle bool` value indicates whether the QueueSet\n107: \t// was idle when the value was calculated, but might no longer be\n108: \t// accurate by the time the client examines that value.\n109: \tFinish(execute func()) (idle bool)\n110: }\n111: \n112: // QueuingConfig defines the configuration of the queuing aspect of a QueueSet.\n113: type QueuingConfig struct {\n114: \t// Name is used to identify a queue set, allowing for descriptive information about its intended use\n115: \tName string\n116: \n117: \t// DesiredNumQueues is the number of queues that the API says\n118: \t// should exist now.  This may be non-positive, in which case\n119: \t// QueueLengthLimit, and HandSize are ignored.\n120: \t// A value of zero means to respect the ConcurrencyLimit of the DispatchingConfig.\n121: \t// A negative value means to always dispatch immediately upon arrival\n122: \t// (i.e., the requests are \"exempt\" from limitation).\n123: \tDesiredNumQueues int\n124: \n125: \t// QueueLengthLimit is the maximum number of requests that may be waiting in a given queue at a time\n126: \tQueueLengthLimit int\n127: \n128: \t// HandSize is a parameter of shuffle sharding.  Upon arrival of a request, a queue is chosen by randomly\n129: \t// dealing a \"hand\" of this many queues and then picking one of minimum length.\n130: \tHandSize int\n131: }\n132: \n133: // DispatchingConfig defines the configuration of the dispatching aspect of a QueueSet.\n134: type DispatchingConfig struct {\n135: \t// ConcurrencyLimit is the maximum number of requests of this QueueSet that may be executing at a time\n136: \tConcurrencyLimit int\n137: \n138: \t// ConcurrencyDenominator is used in relative metrics of concurrency.\n139: \t// It equals ConcurrencyLimit except when that is zero.\n140: \tConcurrencyDenominator int\n141: }\n142: ",

plState.seatDemandStats.highWatermark))\n421: \t\t\tidxOfNonExempt[plName] = len(items)\n422: \t\t\tnonExemptPLNames = append(nonExemptPLNames, plName)\n423: \t\t\titems = append(items, plState.seatDemandStats.smoothed),\n427: \t\t\t})\n428: \t\t\tminCLSum += plState.minCL\n429: \t\t\tminCurrentCLSum += minCurrentCL\n430: \t\t}\n431: \t}\n432: \tif len(items) == 0 &&
